# Grafana Unified Alerting Architecture Overview

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in grafana/grafana that implement the unified alerting (ngalert) subsystem: the alert rule storage, the scheduler, the state manager, the notifier, and the history writer. Map the major components and their interactions.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the org domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec.

The subsystem lives entirely under `pkg/services/ngalert/` and comprises ~270 Go source files across 15+ packages:

Helper types: models.go, compat.go, deltas.go, transactions.go, range_to_instant.go.\\n\\n**Scheduler** (schedule/): Drives periodic evaluation. schedule.go is the main loop; alert_rule.go is the per-alert-rule goroutine; recording_rule.go handles recording rules; registry.go tracks active rule goroutines; fetcher.go loads rules from storage; jitter.go, retry.go, sequence.go, and ticker/ provide timing utilities; loaded_metrics_reader.go provides metrics.\\n\\n**State Manager** (state/): manager.go processes evaluation results and drives state transitions. cache.go holds in-memory state. state.go defines the State type. persist.go, persister_async.go, persister_noop.go, persister_sync.go, and persister_sync_rule.go implement state persistence strategies. multi_instance_reader.go, compat.go, and template/ support state evaluation.\\n\\n**History Writer / Historian** (state/historian/): Records state-change history. backend.go defines the Historian interface. annotation.go writes to Grafana annotations, loki.go writes to remote Loki, prometheus.go writes to Prometheus, multiple.go fans out to multiple backends, noop.go is a no-op. model/ contains the history rule model; core.go and dashboard.go are shared utilities; query.go handles history queries.\\n\\n**Notifier** (notifier/): multiorg_alertmanager.go manages per-org Alertmanager instances. alertmanager.go wraps the embedded Alertmanager. autogen_alertmanager.go auto-generates default configs. redis_peer.go/redis_channel.go provide Redis HA clustering. silence_svc.go and receiver_svc.go manage silences and receivers. legacy_storage/ handles legacy config persistence. crypto.go, file_store.go, images.go, templates.go, sender.go, validation.go are supporting components.\\n\\n**Remote Alertmanager** (remote/): Supports remote Mimir-based Alertmanager. remote_primary_forked_alertmanager.go and remote_secondary_forked_alertmanager.go implement forked modes. client/ contains the Mimir API client (alertmanager.go, alertmanager_configuration.go, alertmanager_state.go, mimir.go, mimir_auth_round_tripper.go).\\n\\n**Sender** (sender/): router.go routes alerts to internal or external Alertmanagers. sender.go implements ExternalAlertmanager for sending to external AMs. notifier.go and notifier_ext.go integrate with the Prometheus notifier library. slog_adapter.go bridges logging.\\n\\n**Evaluator** (eval/): eval.go implements ConditionEval for alert rule conditions. validate.go validates conditions. context.go holds evaluation context. extract_md.go extracts metadata.\\n\\n**Models** (models/): Shared data types: alert_rule.go, alert_query.go, instance.go, instance_labels.go, alertmanager.go, provisioning.go, silence.go, receivers.go, notifications.go, history.go, image.go, admin_configuration.go, permissions.go, accesscontrol.go, constants.go, errors.go, fingerprint.go, time.go.\\n\\n**API** (api/): REST API layer. api_alertmanager.go, api_ruler.go, api_provisioning.go, api_configuration.go, api_testing.go, api_convert_prometheus.go, api_ruler_history.go, api_ruler_export.go, api_alertmanager_silences.go implement endpoints. forking_alertmanager.go, forking_ruler.go, forking_prometheus.go handle routing. lotex_am.go, lotex_ruler.go, lotex_prom.go proxy to remote data sources. generated_base_api_*.go are auto-generated stubs. tooling/definitions/ contains OpenAPI type definitions. compat/, hcl/, prometheus/, validation/ are sub-packages.\\n\\n**Provisioning** (provisioning/): alert_rules.go, contactpoints.go, templates.go, mute_timings.go, notification_policies.go implement the provisioning API services. validation/ checks provenance. compat.go bridges formats.\\n\\n**Supporting packages**: image/ (screenshot capture service), metrics/ (Prometheus metrics for all subsystems), accesscontrol/ (RBAC for rules, receivers, silences), backtesting/ (rule backtesting engine), prom/ (Prometheus rule format conversion), lokiconfig/ (Loki client configuration), tests/ and testutil/ (integration test utilities and fakes).\"\n}\n",

provide timing utilities; loaded_metrics_reader.go provides metrics.\\n\\n**State Manager** (state/): manager.go processes evaluation results and drives state transitions. cache.go holds in-memory multi_instance_reader.go, compat.go, and template/ support state evaluation.\\n\\n**History Writer / Historian** (state/historian/): Records state-change history. backend.go defines the Historian interface. annotation.go writes to Grafana annotations, loki.go writes to remote Loki, prometheus.go writes to Prometheus, multiple.go fans out to multiple backends, noop.go is a no-op. model/ contains the history rule model; core.go and dashboard.go are shared utilities; query.go handles history queries.\\n\\n**Notifier** (notifier/): multiorg_alertmanager.go manages per-org Alertmanager instances. alertmanager.go wraps the embedded Alertmanager. autogen_alertmanager.go auto-generates default configs. redis_peer.go/redis_channel.go provide Redis HA clustering. silence_svc.go and receiver_svc.go manage silences and receivers. legacy_storage/ handles legacy config persistence. crypto.go, file_store.go, images.go, templates.go, sender.go, validation.go are supporting components.\\n\\n**Remote Alertmanager** (remote/): Supports remote Mimir-based Alertmanager. remote_primary_forked_alertmanager.go and remote_secondary_forked_alertmanager.go implement forked modes. client/ contains the Mimir API client (alertmanager.go, alertmanager_configuration.go, alertmanager_state.go, mimir.go, mimir_auth_round_tripper.go).\\n\\n**Sender** (sender/): router.go routes alerts to internal or external Alertmanagers. sender.go implements ExternalAlertmanager for sending to external AMs. notifier.go and notifier_ext.go integrate with the Prometheus notifier library. slog_adapter.go bridges logging.\\n\\n**Evaluator** (eval/): eval.go implements ConditionEval for alert rule conditions. validate.go validates conditions. context.go holds evaluation context. extract_md.go extracts metadata.\\n\\n**Models** (models/): Shared data types: alert_rule.go, alert_query.go, instance.go, instance_labels.go, alertmanager.go, provisioning.go, silence.go, implement endpoints. forking_alertmanager.go, forking_ruler.go, forking_prometheus.go handle routing. lotex_am.go, lotex_ruler.go, lotex_prom.go proxy to remote data sources. generated_base_api_*.go
